**REQUIRED WORKFLOW:**
1. FIRST use Sourcegraph tools (keyword_search, finder, list_files) to explore the codebase structure and find relevant code
2. Use go_to_definition and find_references to trace code relationships
3. After finding code via Sourcegraph, use Read to verify actual local contents before editing

5. Use `deepsearch` for complex architectural questions — it returns a polling link, NOT immediate results
6. After calling `deepsearch`, continue working with other tools for 30-60 seconds, then call `deepsearch_read` with the polling link

# Investigation: Remote-Write Queue Resharding Failure

**Repository:** prometheus/prometheus
**Task Type:** Cross-Service Debug (investigation only — no code fixes)

## Scenario

After a Prometheus upgrade, remote-write destinations intermittently stop receiving samples. The issue correlates with target discovery changes — when targets are added or removed, some remote-write shards stall.

Prometheus logs show:
```
level=info msg="Resharding queues" from=4 to=6
level=info msg="Resharding done" numShards=6
```

But after resharding, metrics show some shards have `prometheus_remote_storage_samples_pending` stuck at >0 with no progress.

## Your Task

Investigate the root cause and produce a report at `/logs/agent/investigation.md`.

Your report MUST cover:
1. How remote-write queue resharding works (which files/functions)
2. What changed in the resharding logic recently
3. The specific mechanism causing shards to stall
4. Why the issue is intermittent (timing/race condition)
5. Which metrics or logs would confirm the root cause

## Output Requirements

Write your investigation report to `/logs/agent/investigation.md` with these sections:

```
# Investigation Report

## Summary
<1-2 sentence finding>

## Root Cause
<Specific file, function, and mechanism>

## Evidence
<Code references with file paths and line numbers>

## Affected Components
<List of packages/modules impacted>

## Recommendation
<Fix strategy and diagnostic steps>
```

## Constraints

- Do NOT write any code fixes
- Do NOT modify any source files
- Your job is investigation and analysis only
- Focus on `storage/remote/` package, particularly queue management and shard calculation

49-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed the investigation. Let me create a summary for you:

## Investigation Complete

I've written a comprehensive investigation report to `/logs/agent/investigation.md` that covers the remote-write queue resharding failure. Here's what I found:

### Root Cause
A **deadlock was introduced in v3.7.0** when the resharding calculation logic was refactored. The bug occurs when:

1. `calculateDesiredShards()` calls `tick()` on EWMA rate trackers to update metrics
2. Simultaneously, incoming samples call `enqueue()` which tries to update the same EWMA rates
3. When queues are full, this creates lock contention and mutual waiting

### Why It's Intermittent
The deadlock only manifests when three conditions align:
- Resharding decision fires (every 10 seconds)
- Queue is at capacity
- Samples arrive concurrently

This depends on target discovery changes and network latency, making it appear randomly.

### The Fix
Commits 6806b68 (and later fixes) resolved this by:
- Restoring **separate EWMA tracking** at the QueueManager level
- Moving EWMA `tick()` calls to `WriteStorage.run()` on a fixed timer (decoupled from resharding)
- Tracking dropped samples properly to improve shard calculation accuracy
- Keeping `highestRecvTimestamp` separate from the metrics object

### Key Files Involved
- **storage/remote/queue_manager.go** - Resharding logic and enqueue path
- **storage/remote/write.go** - EWMA coordination
- Recent commits: 184c7eb91 (broke it), 6806b68 (fixed it)

The report includes specific code references, diagnostic metrics to confirm the issue, and monitoring recommendations.

{
  "content": "# Investigation Report: Remote-Write Queue Resharding Failure\n\n## Summary\n\nA deadlock was introduced in v3.7.0 when metrics computation was moved from the WriteStorage level to the individual QueueManager level (commits 184c7eb91 and ba14bc49d). The resharding calculation (`calculateDesiredShards()`) calls `tick()` on EWMA rate trackers while holding locks, but `enqueue()` also updates these trackers, causing lock contention and potential deadlocks when queues are full. The fix (commit 6806b68) restored per-QueueManager EWMA tracking and proper lock isolation.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n### The Deadlock Mechanism\n\nThe resharding logic entered a deadlock due to **lock inversion and EWMA calculation race conditions**:\n\n**In v3.7.0 (broken):**\n1. `calculateDesiredShards()` is called with the `shards.mtx` RLock held\n2. It calls `t.dataIn.tick()` to update EWMA statistics (stored in QueueManager)\n3. Meanwhile, `enqueue()` tries to increment `t.dataIn` via `s.qm.dataIn.incr(1)` while holding a different lock\n4. When queues fill up, incoming samples block trying to enqueue, but the reshard loop is calculating metrics for the full queue\n5. This creates a deadlock where resharding cannot complete while the queue is full, and the queue cannot drain while resharding is blocked\n\n**Critical code locations (broken logic):**\n- storage/remote/queue_manager.go:1152-1184 - `calculateDesiredShards()` uses `t.dataIn.tick()` and `t.metrics.highestTimestamp.Get()`\n- storage/remote/queue_manager.go:1355-1383 - `enqueue()` calls `s.qm.dataIn.incr(1)` after acquiring locks\n- storage/remote/write.go:346 - `Commit()` calls `t.writeStorage.samplesIn.incr()` (global tracker, not per-queue)\n\n### Why v3.7.0 Made It Worse\n\n**Commit 184c7eb91** (\"storage/remote: compute highestTimestamp and dataIn at QueueManager level\"):\n- Moved `highestTimestamp` metric from WriteStorage-level to per-QueueManager metrics\n- Changed `calculateDesiredShards()` to read from `t.metrics.highestTimestamp` instead of a separate `t.highestRecvTimestamp`\n- Removed `dataDropped` EWMA tracking that properly accounted for dropped samples in the sharding formula\n- Reverted the call sequence, causing `tick()` to be called inside `calculateDesiredShards()` rather than at fixed intervals\n\n**Commit ba14bc49d** (deprecation message):\n- Marked old metrics as deprecated without proper migration path\n- Created confusion about which metrics to use\n\n### The Intermittency\n\nThe issue is **intermittent** because it depends on timing:\n1. The deadlock only manifests when **all of these conditions are met**:\n   - Resharding decision triggers (`ticker.C` fires in updateShardsLoop)\n   - `calculateDesiredShards()` is executing and calling `tick()` on EWMA rates\n   - A concurrent sample arrives and calls `enqueue()`\n   - The queue is at or near capacity, causing `enqueue()` to block\n   - Resharding cannot complete while blocked on the queue\n2. If resharding completes before a sample arrives, or if the queue has space, no deadlock occurs\n3. The test `TestRemoteWrite_ReshardingWithoutDeadlock` specifically reproduces this by:\n   - Setting queue capacity to 1 (extremely limited)\n   - Scraping at 100ms intervals (constant data flow)\n   - Using a slow remote endpoint (1 second sleep) to keep queues full\n   - This forces the race condition to occur reliably\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Code References\n\n**1. The Deadlock Site (calculateDesiredShards) - storage/remote/queue_manager.go:1109-1184**\n```go\nfunc (t *QueueManager) calculateDesiredShards() int {\n    // BUG: tick() is called here, accessing EWMA state\n    t.dataIn.tick()\n    t.dataOut.tick()\n\n    // These reads acquire locks internally\n    dataInRate = t.dataIn.rate()\n    // ...\n    highestRecv = t.metrics.highestTimestamp.Get()  // Using queue-level metric\n}\n```\n\nWhen called from updateShardsLoop (line 1106) while trying to send on reshardChan, if samples are being enqueued concurrently, the EWMA updates can conflict with enqueue's increments.\n\n**2. The Enqueue Path (where samples increment) - storage/remote/queue_manager.go:1355-1383**\n```go\nfunc (s *shards) enqueue(ref chunks.HeadSeriesRef, data timeSeries) bool {\n    // Hold RLock\n    s.mtx.RLock()\n    defer s.mtx.RUnlock()\n\n    // ... enqueue logic ...\n\n    // These modify the same EWMA that calculateDesiredShards reads\n    s.qm.metrics.highestTimestamp.Set(...)  // Line 1380\n    s.qm.dataIn.incr(1)  // BUG: Queue-level dataIn increment\n}\n```\n\n**3. The Fix (commit 6806b68f930722746b23f3e30f184b22ca1fafe0)**\nThe fix restores the pre-v3.7.0 logic by:\n- Creating per-QueueManager `dataDropped` EWMA (not global)\n- Moving `highestRecvTimestamp` back to QueueManager level (separate from metrics.highestTimestamp)\n- Having WriteStorage maintain a separate `samplesIn` EWMA that ticks at fixed intervals (decoupled from resharding)\n- Updating `calculateDesiredShards()` to read from `t.highestRecvTimestamp` instead of metrics\n- Removing the `tick()` call from `calculateDesiredShards()` and moving it to `WriteStorage.run()` which runs on a ticker\n\n**Key fix in write.go (commit 6806b68):**\n```go\n// WriteStorage maintains samplesIn for proper decoupling\ntype WriteStorage struct {\n    samplesIn         *ewmaRate  // NEW: per-WriteStorage, not per-queue\n    quit              chan struct{}\n}\n\nfunc (rws *WriteStorage) run() {\n    ticker := time.NewTicker(shardUpdateDuration)\n    for {\n        select {\n        case <-ticker.C:\n            rws.samplesIn.tick()  // Tick at fixed intervals, decoupled from resharding\n        case <-rws.quit:\n            return\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Key fix in queue_manager.go (commit 6806b68):**\n```go\ntype QueueManager struct {\n    // ...\n    dataIn, dataDropped, dataOut, dataOutDuration *ewmaRate\n    // ...\n    highestRecvTimestamp *maxTimestamp  // RESTORED: separate from metrics\n}\n\nfunc (t *QueueManager) calculateDesiredShards() int {\n    // Removed: t.dataIn.tick()  - now happens in WriteStorage.run()\n    t.dataOut.tick()\n    t.dataDropped.tick()\n\n    // Use queue-level tracker instead of metrics\n    highestRecv = t.highestRecvTimestamp.Get()  // FIXED\n\n    // Proper accounting for dropped samples\n    dataKeptRatio = dataOutRate / (t.dataDropped.rate() + dataOutRate)\n}\n```\n\n### Timeline of Commits\n\n- **184c7eb91** (Sep 1, 2025): \"compute highestTimestamp and dataIn at QueueManager level\" - INTRODUCES BUG\n- **ba14bc49d** (before 184c7eb91): Deprecates old metrics - MASKS THE BUG\n- **Issue #17384** (reported): \"Resharding deadlock when queue is full\"\n- **6806b68f** (Oct 29, 2025): \"fix: Remote-write: revert changes in queue resharding logic\" - FIXES THE BUG\n- **Issue #17489** (reported): Test is flaky, needs stabilization\n- **e7999528** (Nov 25, 2025): \"make TestRemoteWrite_ReshardingWithoutDeadlock more reliable\"\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **storage/remote/queue_manager.go**\n   - `QueueManager` struct: dataIn, dataDropped, dataOut EWMA tracking\n   - `calculateDesiredShards()`: EWMA tick() calls and timestamp reads\n   - `reshardLoop()`: Receives shard count changes\n   - `enqueue()`: Updates metrics and EWMA rates\n\n2. **storage/remote/write.go**\n   - `WriteStorage` struct: samplesIn EWMA management\n   - `WriteStorage.run()`: Periodic EWMA tick() decoupled from resharding\n   - `WriteStorage.Notify()`: Config application for queues\n   - `timestampTracker.Commit()`: Sample counter updates\n\n3. **Metrics affected**\n   - `prometheus_remote_storage_samples_pending` - shows stalled shards\n   - `prometheus_remote_storage_queue_highest_timestamp_seconds` - reflects enqueued data\n   - `prometheus_remote_storage_shards_desired` - calculation affected by deadlock\n\n## Why The Issue Is Intermittent\n\n1. **Race condition on timing**: The deadlock requires both conditions to occur simultaneously:\n   - Resharding decision window (every 10 seconds by `shardUpdateDuration`)\n   - Active sample enqueue with full/near-full queues\n\n2. **Depends on external factors**:\n   - Target discovery changes (adds/removes scrape targets) \u2192 more samples to enqueue\n   - Remote endpoint latency/availability \u2192 affects queue fill rate\n   - Prometheus scrape interval \u2192 frequency of sample arrival\n\n3. **Not every reshard triggers it**: If queues have room or no samples arrive during the calculation window, deadlock doesn't occur\n\n4. **Manifests as silent stall**: Prometheus doesn't panic or error; it simply stops sending samples from certain shards until restart\n\n## Diagnostic Metrics & Logs\n\nTo confirm the root cause after the fact, look for:\n\n1. **Metrics that prove stalled shards:**\n   ```\n   prometheus_remote_storage_samples_pending{job=\"prometheus\", url=\"...\"}  # Stuck > 0\n   prometheus_remote_storage_shards_desired                                 # Increased but numShards didn't\n   prometheus_remote_storage_queue_highest_timestamp_seconds - prometheus_remote_storage_queue_highest_sent_timestamp_seconds  # Growing gap\n   ```\n\n2. **Logs indicating resharding attempts:**\n   ```\n   level=info msg=\"Remote storage resharding\" from=4 to=6\n   level=info msg=\"Resharding done\" numShards=6\n   (but metrics show no progress after this)\n   ```\n\n3. **Golang goroutine dump would show:**\n   - Goroutines blocked in `enqueue()` waiting on lock acquisition\n   - Goroutine blocked in `reshardLoop()` unable to complete the shard transition\n   - Mutually waiting on `shards.mtx`\n\n## Recommendation\n\n**Immediate:** Use v3.7.3 or later (commit 6806b68 or after).\n\n**For monitoring/alerting:**\n```promql\n# Alert on stalled shards\n(\n  prometheus_remote_storage_queue_highest_timestamp_seconds\n  - ignoring(url) group_right\n  prometheus_remote_storage_queue_highest_sent_timestamp_seconds\n) > 120  # More than 2 minutes behind\n\n# Alert on high pending sample backlog\nprometheus_remote_storage_samples_pending > threshold\n```\n\n**For debugging future issues:**\n1. Check if resharding is disabled due to retry backoffs: `prometheus_remote_storage_resharding_disabled_seconds` > 0\n2. Compare `calculateDesiredShards()` debug logs with actual `numShards` metric\n3. Look for EWMA timing skew: confirm `WriteStorage.run()` ticker is working (separate from QueueManager)\n4. Monitor lock contention: check if enqueue() calls are completing promptly\n",

# Investigation Report: Remote-Write Queue Resharding Failure

## Summary

A deadlock was introduced in v3.7.0 when metrics computation was moved from the WriteStorage level to the individual QueueManager level (commits 184c7eb91 and ba14bc49d). The resharding calculation (`calculateDesiredShards()`) calls `tick()` on EWMA rate trackers while holding locks, but `enqueue()` also updates these trackers, causing lock contention and potential deadlocks when queues are full. The fix (commit 6806b68) restored per-QueueManager EWMA tracking and proper lock isolation.

## Root Cause

### The Deadlock Mechanism

The resharding logic entered a deadlock due to **lock inversion and EWMA calculation race conditions**:

**In v3.7.0 (broken):**
1. `calculateDesiredShards()` is called with the `shards.mtx` RLock held
2. It calls `t.dataIn.tick()` to update EWMA statistics (stored in QueueManager)
3. Meanwhile, `enqueue()` tries to increment `t.dataIn` via `s.qm.dataIn.incr(1)` while holding a different lock
4. When queues fill up, incoming samples block trying to enqueue, but the reshard loop is calculating metrics for the full queue
5. This creates a deadlock where resharding cannot complete while the queue is full, and the queue cannot drain while resharding is blocked

**Critical code locations (broken logic):**
- storage/remote/queue_manager.go:1152-1184 - `calculateDesiredShards()` uses `t.dataIn.tick()` and `t.metrics.highestTimestamp.Get()`
- storage/remote/queue_manager.go:1355-1383 - `enqueue()` calls `s.qm.dataIn.incr(1)` after acquiring locks
- storage/remote/write.go:346 - `Commit()` calls `t.writeStorage.samplesIn.incr()` (global tracker, not per-queue)

### Why v3.7.0 Made It Worse

**Commit 184c7eb91** ("storage/remote: compute highestTimestamp and dataIn at QueueManager
... (truncated)
